58b6('bum): ma dang bral ba'i sems kyis tshul khrims srungs pa dang / mtshan ma dang bral ba'i sems kyis bzod pa sgrub pa dang / mtshan ma dang bral ba'i sems kyis brtson 'grus rtsom pa dang / mtshan ma dang bral
58b7('bum): ba'i sems kyis bsam gtan la mnyam par gzhog pa dang / mtsham dang bral ba'i sems kyis shes rab sgom pa dang / mtshan ma dang bral ba'i sems kyis nang stong pa nyid sgom pa dang / mtshan
58b8('bum): ma dang bral ba'i sems kyis phyi stong pa nyid sgom pa dang / mtshan ma dang bral ba'i sems kyis phyi nang stong pa nyid sgom pa dang / mtshan ma dang bral ba'i sems kyi stong pa nyid stong pa nyid sgom pa dang / mtshan
59a1('bum): ma dang bral ba'i sems kyis chen po stong pa nyid sgom pa dang / mtshan ma dang bral ba'i sems kyis don dam pa stong pa nyid sgom pa dang / mtshan ma dang bral ba'i sems kyis
59a2('bum): 'das byas stong pa nyid sgom pa dang / mtshan ma dang bral ba'i sems kyis 'dus ma byas stong pa nyid sgom pa dang / mtshan ma dang bral ba'i sems kyis mtha' las 'das pa stong pa nyid sgom pa dang / 
59a3('bum): mtshan ma dang bral ba'i sems kyis thog ma dang tha ma med pa stong pa nyid sgom pa dang / mtshan ma dang bral ba'i sems kyis dor ba med pa stong pa nyid bsgom pa dang / mtshan ma dang bral ba'i
59a4('bum): sems kyis rang bzhin stong pa nyid sgom pa dang / mtshan ma dang dbral ba'i sems kyis chos thams cad stong pa nyid sgom pa dang / mtshan ma dang bral ba'i sems kyis rang gi mtshan nyid
59a5('bum): stong pa nyid sgom pa dang / mtshan ma dang bral ba'i sems kyis/ mi dmigs pa stong pa nyid sgom pa dang / mtshan ma dang bral ba'i sems kyis dngos po med pa stong pa nyid sgom pa dang
59a6('bum): mtshan ma dang bral ba'i sems kyis ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid sgom pa dang / mtshan ma dang bral ba'i sems kyis dngos po med pa'i ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid sgom pa dang / mtshan ma dang bral ba'i sems kyis dran
59a7('bum): pa nye bar gzhag pa rnams sgom pa dang / mtshan ma dang bral ba'i sems kyis yang dag par spong ba rnams sgom pa dang / mtshan ma dang bral ba'i sems kyis rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa rnams sgom pa dang
59a8('bum): mtshan ma dang bral ba'i sems kyis dbang po rnams sgom pa dang / mtshan ma dang bral ba'i sems kyis stobs rnams sgom pa dang / mtshan ma dang bral ba'i sems kyis byang chub kyi
59b1('bum): yan lag rnams sgom pa dang / mtshan ma dang bral ba'i sems kyis 'phags pa'i lam yan lag brgyad pa sgom pa dang / mtshan ma dang bral ba'i sems kyis 'phags pa'i bden pa rnams sgom/ 
59b2('bum): pa dang / mtshan ma dang bral ba'i sems kyis bsam gtan rnams sgom pa dang / mtshan ma dang bral ba'i sems kyis tshad med pa rnams sgom pa dang / mtshan ma dang bral ba'i
59b3('bum): sems kyis gzugs med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa rnams sgom pa dang / mtshan ma dang bral ba'i sems kyis rnam par thar pa rnams sgom pa dang / mtshan ma dang bral ba'i sems kyis
59b4('bum): mthar kyis gnas pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa rnams sgom par / mtshan ma dang bral ba'i sems kyis rnam par thar pa'i sgo stong pa nyid dang / mtshan ma med pa dang / smon pa med pasgom
59b5('bum): pa dang / mtshan ma dang bral ba'i sems kyis mngon par shes pa rnams sgom pa dang / mtshan ma dang bral ba'isems kyis ting 'dzin rnams sgom pa dang / mtshan ma dang
59b6('bum): bral ba'i sems kyis gzungs kyi sgo rnams sgom pa dang / mtshan ma dang bral ba'i sems kyis de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs rnams sgom pa dang / mtshan ma dang bral ba'i sems kyis mi
59b7('bum): 'jigs pa rnams sgom pa dang / mtshan ma dang bral ba'i sems kyis so so yang dag par rig pa rnams sgom pa dang / mtshan ma dang bral ba'i sems kyis byams pa chen po sgom pa dang / 
59b8('bum): mtshan ma dang bral ba'i sems kyis snying rje chen po sgom pa dang / mtshan ma dang bral ba'i sems kyis sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa rnams sgom pa dang / mtshan ma dang bral ba'i sems kyis
60a1('bum): rgyun tu zhugs pa'i 'bras bu sgom pa dang / mtshan ma dang bral ba'i sems kyis lan cig phyir ba'i 'bras bu sgom pa dang / mtshan ma dang bral ba'i sems kyis phyir mi 'ong ba'i 'bras
60a2('bum): bu sgom pa dang / mtshan ma dang bral ba'i sems kyis dgra bcom pa nyid sgom pa dang / mtshan ma dang bral ba'i sems kyis rang byang chub sgom pa dang / mtshan ma dang bral ba'i sems kyis lam gyi rnam pa
60a3('bum): shes pa nyid sgom pa dang / mtshan ma dang bral ba'i sems kyis rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid sgom pa 'di ni/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i thabs mkhas pa'o// gsol pa/ 
60a4('bum): bcom ldan 'das bdag gis bcom ldan 'das kyis gsung ngas pa'i don 'tshal ba ltar na/ byang chub sems dang / 'a sems dpa' chen po sems dang po bskyed pa nas nye bar bzung
60a5('bum): ste/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa dang / thabs mkhas pa dang ma bral na/ de'i bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub ni the tsom ma mchis so// de ci'i
60a6('bum): phyir zhe na/ bcom ldan 'das de ni 'di ltar/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po des/ sems dang po bskyed pa nas nye bar bzung ste/ gang mngon par 'tshang rgya ba dang / gang gis
60a7('bum): mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya ba dang / gang mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bar bgyi ba'i gzugs sam/ tsher ba 'am/ 'du shes sam/ 'du byed dam/ rnam par shes pa'am/ 
60a8('bum): mig gam/ rna ba'am/ sna 'am/ lce'am/ lus sam/ yid dam/ gzugs ma/ sgra'am/ dri 'am/ ro 'am/ reg gam/ chos sam/ mig gi rnam par shes pa'am/ rna ba'i
60b1('bum): rnam par shes pa'am/ sna'i rnam par shes pa'am/ lce'i rnam par shes pa 'am/ lus kyi rnam par shes pa'am/ yid kyi rnam par shes pa'am/ mig gi 'dus te reg pa'am/ rnab / 
60b2('bum): 'dus te reg pa'am/ sna'i 'dus te reg pa'am/ lce'i 'dus te reg pa'am/ lus kyi 'dus te reg pa 'am/ yid kyi 'dus te reg pa'am/ mig gi 'dus te reg pa las byung
60b3('bum): ba'i tsher ba 'am/ rna ba'i 'dus te reg pa las byung ba'i tshe raba'am/ sna'i 'dus te reg pa las byung ba'i tshe ba 'am/ lce'i 'dus te reg pa las byung ba'i tshe rab 'am/ lus kyi
60b4('bum): 'dus te reg pa byung ba'i tshe rab 'am/ yid kyi 'dus te reg pa las byung ba'i tsho ba 'am/ sa'i khamasasam/ chu'i khams sam/ me'i khams sam/ rlung
60b5('bum): gi khams sam/ nam mkha'i khams sam/ rnam par shes pa'i khams sam/ ma rig pa'ama'adu byed dam/ rnam par shes pa 'am/ ming dang / 
60b6('bum): gzugs sam/ skye mched drug gam/ reg pa'am/ tshor ba'am/ sred pa'am/ len pa'am/ srid pa 'am/ skye ba'am/ rga shi 'am/ sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa'am/ tshul khrims kyi pha
60b7('bum): rol tu phyin pa'am/ bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa'am/ brtson 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'am/ bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa'am/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu
60b8('bum): phyin pa'am/ nang stong pa nyid dam/ phyi stong pa nyid dam/ phyi nang stong pa nyid dam/ stong pa nyid stong pa nyid dam/ chen po stong pa nyid dam/ don dam pa stong pa nyid dam/ 'dus byas stong
61a1('bum): pa nyid dam/ 'dus ma byas stong pa nyid dam/ mtha' las 'das pa stong pa nyid dam/ thog ma dang tha ma med pa stong pa nyid dam/ dor ba med pa stong pa nyid dam/ rang bzhin stong pa nyid dam/ 
61a2('bum): chos thams cad stong pa nyid dam/ rang gi mtshan nyid stong pa nyid dam/ mi dmigs pa stong pa nyid dam/ dngos po med pa stong pa nyid dam/ ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid dam/ dngos po med pa'i ngo bo
61a3('bum): nyid stong pa nyid dam/ dran pa nye bar gzhag pa rnams sam/ yang dag par spong ba rnams sam/ rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa rnams sam/ dbang po rnams sam/ stobs rnams sam/ byang
61a4('bum): chub kyi yan lag rnams sam 'phags pa'i lam yan lag brgyad pa'am/ 'phags pa'i bden pa rnam sa sam/ bsam gtan rnams sam/ tshad med pa rnams
61a5('bum): dang gzugs med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa rnams sam/ rnam par thar pa rnams sam mthar kyis gnas pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa rnams sam/ rnam par thar
61a6('bum): pa'i sgo stong pa nyid dang / mtshan ma med pa dang / smon pa med pa'am/ mngon par shes pa rnams sam ting 'dzin rnams sam/ gzungs kyi sgo rnams sam/ de bzhin gshes
61a7('bum): pa'i stobs rnams sam/ mi 'jigs pa rnams sam so so yang dag par rig pa rnams sam/ byams pa chen po'am/ snying rje chen po'am/ sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres
61a8('bum): rnams sam/ rgyun tu zhugs pa'i 'bras bu'am/ lan cig phyir 'ong ba'i 'bras bu'am/ phyir mi 'ong ba'i 'bras bu'am dgra bcom pa nyid dam/ rang byang chub bam/ 
61b1('bum): lam gyi rnam pa shes pa nyid dam/ rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid dam/ chos gang yang dmigs pa ma mchis so// bcom ldan 'das byang chub sems dpa'i theg pa pa'i rigs kyi ba'am/ 
61b2('bum): rigs kyi bu mo gang shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa dang / thabs mkhas pa dang bral ba de dag gi bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub ni the tsom mchis par rig par bgyi ba ste/ de
61b3('bum): ci'i slad du zhe na/ bcom ldan 'das de ni 'di ltar byang chub sems dpa'i theg pa pa'i rigs kyi bu'am/ rigs kyi bu mo dag gis sbyin pa ci dang ci btang ba de thams cad mtshan mar bzung ste ba tu
61b4('bum): de bzhin du tshul khrims gang dang gang bsrungs pa dang / bzod pa ci dang ci bsgrubs pa dang / brtson 'grus gang dang dgang brtsams pa dang / bsam gtan gang dang gang la mnyam
61b5('bum): pabar bzhag pa dang / shes rab gang dang gang bsgoms pa de dag thams cad mtshan mar bzung ste bsgoms pas de'i slad du byang chub sems dpa'i theg pa pa'i rigs kyibu
61b6('bum): 'am rigs kyi bu mo de dag gi bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub ni the tsom mchis par rig par bgyi'o// bcom ldan 'das de'i slad du byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen
61b7('bum): po bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bar 'tshal bas shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa dang thabs mkhas pa dang ma bral bar bgyi'o// 
61b8('bum): shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa dang / thabs mkhas pa la gnas te / mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis/ mtshan ma med pa dang ldan pa'i sems kyis sbyin pa yongasu gtang bar bgyi'o// 
62a1('bum): tshul khrims bsrung bar bgyi'o// bzod pa bsgrub par bgyi'o// brtson 'grus brtsam par bgyi'o// bsam gtan la mnyam par gzhag par bgyi'o// shes rab bsgom par bgyin
62a2('bum): nang stong pa nyid la spyad par bgyi'o// phyi stong pa nyid la spyad par bgyi'o// phyi nang stong pa nyid la spyad par bgyi'o// stong pa nyid stong pa nyid la spyad par bgyi'o// chen po stong pa nyid la spyad par bgyi'o// don
62a3('bum): dam pa stong pa nyid la spyad par bgyi'o// 'dus byas stong pa nyid la spyad par bgyi'o// 'dus ma byas stong pa nyid la spyad par bgyi'o// mtha' las 'das pa stong pa nyid la spyad par bgyi'o// thog
62a4('bum): ma dang tha ma med pa stong pa nyid la spyad par bgyi'o// dor ba med pa stong pa nyid la spyad par bgyi'o// rang bzhin stong pa nyid la spyad par bgyi'o// chos thams cad stong pa nyid la spyad par
62a5('bum): bgyi'o// rang gi mtshan nyid stong pa nyid la spyad par bgyi'o// mi dmigs pa stong pa nyid la spyad par bgyi'o// dngos po med pa stong pa nyid la spyad par bgyi'o// ngo bo nyid
62a6('bum): stong pa nyid la spyad par bgyi'o// dngos po med pa'i ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid la spyad par bgyi'o// dran pa nye bar gzhag pa rnams la sbed par bgyi'o// yang dag par spong ba rnams la spyad par
62a7('bum): bgyi'o// rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa rnams la spyad par bgyi'o// dbang po rnams la spyad par bgyi'o// stobs rnams la spyad par bgyi'o// byang chub kyi yan lag rnams la spyad par bgyi'o// 'phags
62a8('bum): pa'i lam yan lag brgyad pa la spyad par bgyi'o// 'phags pa'i bden pa rnams la spyad par bgyi'o// bsam gtan rnams la spyad par bgyi'o// tshad med pa rnams la spyad par bgyi'o// gzugs
62b1('bum): med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa rnams la spyad par bgyi'o// rnam par thar pa rnams la spyad par bgyi'o// mthar gyis gnas pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa rnams la spyad par bgyi'o// rnam par thar pa'i sgo
62b2('bum): stong pa nyid dang / mtshan ma med pa dang / smon pa med pa la spyad par bgyi'o// mngon par shes pa rnams la spyad par bgyi'o// ting nge 'dzin rnams la spyad par bgyi'o// gzungs kyi sgo rnams la
62b3('bum): spyad par bgyi'o// de bzhin gshegs pa'i stolas la spyad par bgyi'o// mi 'jigs pa rnams la spyad par bgyi'o// so so yang dag par rig pa rnams la spyad par bgyi'o// byams pa chen
62b4('bum): po la spyad par bgyi'o// snying rje chen po la smad par bgyi'o// / sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa rnams la spang pabagyi'o// rgyun tu zhugs pa'i 'bras bu la spyad par
62b5('bum): bgyi'o// lan cig phyir 'ong ba'i 'bras bu la smad par bgyi'o// phyir mi 'ong ba'i 'bras bu la spyad par bgyi'o// dgra bcom pa nyid la spyad par bgyi'o// rang byang chub la
62b6('bum): spyad par bgyi'o// lam gyi rnam pa shes pa nyid la spyad par bgyi'o// rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid la spyad par bgyi'o// de nas 'dod pa na spyod pa dang / gzugs na yod pa ni spyod
62b7('bum): po'i lha'i bu de dag gis bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das de ltar byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen pos chos thams cad
62b8('bum): mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bar bgyid la chis de dag kya ma mchis shing mi dmigs pas/ blan med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub ni 'thung bar nga/ 'o// bcom ldan 'das
63a1('bum): kyis bka' stsal pa/ lnga'i bu dag de de bzhin no// de de bzhin te/ lha'i bu dag bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub ni 'byung bar dka'o// lha'i bu dag ngas kyang chos thams cad
63a2('bum): rnam pa thams cad du mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas te/ don dam par na gang mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya ba 'am/ gang gis mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya ba'am/ gang mngon par
63a3('bum): rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bar bya ba'i chos gang yang mi dmigs so// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ lha'i bu dag chos thams cad shin tu rnam par dag pa'i phyir ro// de nas tshe dang ldan pa rab 'byor gyis/ 
63a4('bum): bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// bco dam ldan 'das kyis gang 'di skad du bla na med pa yang dadag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub ni 'byung bar dka'o// zhes
63a5('bum): gsungs pa/ bcom ldan 'das kyis ji ltar gsungs ba'i don bdag gis 'tshal ba dang / bdag gi sems pa ltar na/ bcom ldan 'das bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs
63a6('bum): pa'i byang chub tu mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bar bgyi ba ni mi dka'o// de ci'i slad du zhe na/ bcom ldan 'das de ni 'di ltar gang yang mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya ba ma mchis/ gang gis
63a7('bum): kyang mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgyab ma mchis/ gang yang mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bar bgyi ba ma mchis te/ chos thams cad stong pa la ni gang mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang
63a8('bum): rgya ba dang / gang gis mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya ba dang / gang mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bar bgyi ba'i chos de lta bu ma mchis so// de ci'i slad du zhe na/ bcom ldan 'das de
63b1('bum): ni 'di ltar chos thams cad ni stong pa ste/ chos gang 'phel bar bgyi ba'i slad du'am/ yongasu 'grib par bgyi ba'i slad du sbyin pa yongasu gtong ba'am/ tshul khrims bsrung ba 'am
63b2('bum): bzod pa bsgom pa'am/ brtson 'grus brtsam pa'am/ bsam gtan la mnyam par gzhag pa'am shes rab bsgom pa'am/ nang stong pa nyid bsgom pa'am/ phyi stong pa nyid bsgom
63b3('bum): ba'am/ phyi nang stong pa nyid bsgom pa'am/ stong pa nyid stong pa nyid bsgom pa'am/ chen po stong pa nyid bsgom pa 'am/ don dam pa stong pa nyid bsgom pa dang / 'dus byas stong pa nyid
63b4('bum): bsgom pa'am/ 'dus ma byas stong pa nyid bsgom pa'am mtha' las 'das pa stong pa nyid bsgom pa 'am thog ma dang tha ma med pa stong pa nyid bsgom pa'am dor
63b5('bum): ba med pa stong pa nyid bsgom pa'am/ rang bzhin stong pa nyid bsgom pa dang / chos thams cad stong pa nyid bsgom pa 'am/ rang gi mtshan nyid stong pa nyid bsgom
63b6('bum): ba'am/ mi dmigs pa stong pa nyid bsgom pa 'am/ dngos po med pa stong pa nyid bsgom pa'am ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid bsgom pa 'am/ dngos po med pa'i ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid
63b7('bum): bsgom pa 'am/ dran pa nye bar bzhag pa rnams bsgom pa'am/ yang dag par spong ba rnams bsgom pa'am/ rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa rnams bsgom pa 'am/ dbang po rnams bsgom
63b8('bum): ba'am/ stobs rnams bsgom pa'am byang chub kyi yan lag rnams bsgom pa'am/ 'phags pa'i lam yan lag brgyad pa bsgom pa'am/ 'phags pa'i bden
64a1('bum): pa rnams bsgom pa'am/ bsam gtan rnams bsgom pa'am/ tshad med pa rnams bsgom pa'am/ gzugs med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa rnams bsgom pa 'am rnam par
64a2('bum): thar pa rnams bsgom pa'am/ mthar gyis gnas pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa rnams bsgom pa'am/ rnam par thar pa'i sgo stong pa nyid dang / mtshan ma med pa dang / smon pa med pa bsgom pa
64a3('bum): 'am/ mngon par shes pa rnams bsgom pa 'am/ ting nge 'dzin rnams bsgom pa dang / gzungs kyi sgo rnams bsgom pa 'am/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs rnams bsgom pa'am/ 
64a4('bum): mi 'jigs rnams bsgom pa'am/ so so yang dag dpar rig pa rnams bsgom pa'am/ byams pa chen po bsgom pa'am/ snying rje chen po bsgom pa 'am/ sangs
64a5('bum): rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa rnams bsgom pa'am/ rgyun tu zhugs pa'i 'bras bu bsgom pa'am/ lan cig/ phyir 'ong ba'i 'bras bu bsgom pa'am/ phyir mi 'ong ba'i 'bras
64a6('bum): bu bsgom pa'am/ dgra bcom pa nyid bsgom pa'am/ rang byang chub bsgom pa'am/ lam gyi rnam pa shes pa nyid bsgom pa'am/ rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi don du
64a7('bum): bslab pa'i chos de dag kyang ma mchis ste/ gang mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya ba'am/ gang gis mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya ba'am/ gang mngon par rdzogs par 'chi
64a8('bum): rgya bar bgyi ba'i chos de dag thams cad kyang stong pa ste/ bcom ldan 'das rnam grangs des na/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen pos bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang
64b1('bum): chub tu mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bar sla'o// de ci'i slad du zhe na/ bcom ldan 'das de ni 'di ltar/ gzugs ni gzugs kyi rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // tshor ba ni tshor ba'i rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // 
64b2('bum): 'du shes ni 'du shes kyi rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // 'du byed ni 'du byed kyi rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // rnam par shes pa ni rnam par shes pa'i rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // mig ni mig gi rang bzhin
64b3('bum): gyis stong ngo // rna ba ni rna ba'i rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // sna ni sna'i rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // lce ni lce'i rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // lus ni lus kyi rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // yid ni yid kyi
64b4('bum): rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // gzugs ni gzugs kyi rang nga bzhin gyis stong ngo // sgra ni sgra'i rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // da/ dri ni dri'i rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // ro ni ro'i rang bzhin gyis
64b5('bum): stong ngo // reg ni reg gi rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // chos ni chos kyi rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // mig gi rnam par shes pa ni mig gi rnam par shes pa'i rang bzhin gyis
64b6('bum): stong ngo // rna ba'i rnam par shes pa ni rna ba'i rnam par shes pa'i rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // sna'i rnam par shes pa ni sna'i rnam par shes pa'i rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // lce'i rnam par shes
64b7('bum): pa ni lce'i rnam par shes pa'i rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // lus kyi rnam par shes pa ni lus kyi rnam par shes pa'i rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // yid kyi rnam par shes pa ni yid kyi rnam par shes
64b8('bum): pa'i rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // mig gi 'dus te reg pa ni mig gi 'dus te reg pa'i rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // rna ba'i 'dus te reg pa ni rna ba'i 'dus te reg pa'i rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // 
65a1('bum): sna'i 'dus te reg pa ni sna'i 'dus te reg pa'i rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // lce'i 'dus te reg pa ni lce'i 'dus te reg pa'i rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // 
65a2('bum): lus kyi 'dus te reg pa ni lus kyi 'dus te reg pa'i rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // yid kyi 'dus te reg pa ni yid kyi 'dus te reg pa'i rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // mig gi 'dus te
65a3('bum): reg pa las byung ba'i tsher ba ni mig gi 'dus te reg pa las byung ba'i tsher ba'i rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // rna ba'i 'dus te reg pa las byung ba'i tshe rab ni rna ba'i 'dus te reg pa
65a4('bum): las byung ba'i tshor ba'i rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // sna'i 'dus te reg pa las byung ba'i tshe ra ba ni sna'i 'dus te reg pra las byung ba'i tshor ba'i rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // 
65a5('bum): lce'i 'dus te reg pa las byung ba'i tsher ba ni lce'i 'dus/ te reg pa las byung ba'i tshor ba'i rang bzhin gyis/ stong ngo // lus kyi 'dus te reg pa las byung ba'i
65a6('bum): tshor ba ni lus kyi 'dus te reg pa las byung ba'i tshor ba'i rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // yid kyi 'dus te reg pa la sa byung ba'i tsher ba ni yid kyi 'dus te reg pa las byung
65a7('bum): ba'i tshor ba'i rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // sa'i khams ni sa'i khams kyi rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // chu'i khams ni chu'i khams kyi rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // me'i
65a8('bum): khams ni me'i khams kyi rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // rlung gi khams ni rlung gi khams kyi rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // nam mkha'i khams ni namakha'i khams kyi rang bzhin/ 
65b1('bum): gyis stong ngo // rnam par shes pa'i khams ni rnam par shes pa'i khams kyi rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // ma rig pa ni ma rig pa'i rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // 
65b2('bum): 'du byed ni 'du byed kyi rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // rnam par shes pa ni rnam par shes pa'i rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // ming dang gzugs ni ming dang gzugs kyi rang bzhin gyis
65b3('bum): stong ngo // skye mched drug ni skye mched drug gi rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // reg pa ni reg pa'i rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // tshor ba ni tsher ba'i rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // sred
65b4('bum): ba ni sred pa'i rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // len pa/ ni len pa'i rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // srid pa da ni srid pa'i rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // skye ba ni skye ba'i
65b5('bum): rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // rga shi na rga shi'i rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyinapa ni sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa'i rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // 
65b6('bum): tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ni tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa ni bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa'i rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // 
65b7('bum): brtson 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ni brtson 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa ni bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i
66a1('bum): rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ni shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // nang stong pa nyid ni nang stong pa
66a2('bum): nyid kyi rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // phyi stong pa nyid ni phyi stong pa nyid kyi rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // phyi nang stong pa nyid ni phyi nang stong pa nyid kyi rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // stong pa nyid stong
66a3('bum): pa nyid ni stong pa nyid stong pa nyid kyi rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // chen po stong pa nyid ni chen po stong pa nyid kyi rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // don dam pa stong pa nyid ni don dam pa stong pa nyid
66a4('bum): kyi rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // 'dus byas stong pa nyid ni dus byas stong pa nyid kyi rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // 'dus ma byas stong pa nyid ni 'dus ma byas stong pa nyid kyi rang
66a5('bum): bzhin gyis stong ngo // mtha' las 'das pa ste/ nga pa nyid ni mtha' las 'das pa stong pa nyid kyi rang / bzhin gyis stong ngo // thog ma dang tha ma med pa stong
66a6('bum): pa nyid ni thog ma dang tha ma med pa stong pa nyid kyi rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // dor ba med pa stong pa nyid ni dor ba med pa stong pa nyid kyi rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // rang bzhin stong pa nyid
66a7('bum): ni rang bzhin stong pa nyid kyi rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // chos thams cad stong pa nyid ni chos thams cad stong pa nyid kyi rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // rang gi mtshan nyid stong pa nyid
66a8('bum): ni rang gi mtshan nyid stong pa nyid kyi rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // mi dmigs pa stong pa nyid ni mi dmigs pa stong pa nyid kyi rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // dngos po med pa stong pa nyid ni dngos po
66b1('bum): med pa stong pa nyid kyi rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid ni ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid kyi rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // dngos po med pa'i ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid ni dngos po med pa'i ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid
66b2('bum): kyi rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // dran pa nye bar bzhag pa rnams ni dran pa nye bar bzhag pa'i rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // yang dag par spong ba rnams ni yang dag par spong ba'i rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // / 
66b3('bum): rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa rnams ni rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa'i rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // dbang po rnams ni dbang po'i rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // stobs rnams ni stobs kyi rang
66b4('bum): bzhin gyis stong ngo // byang chub kyi yan lag rnams ni byang chub kyi yan lag gi rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // 'phags pa'i lam yan lag brgyad pa ni 'phags pa'i
66b5('bum): lam yan lag brgyad pa'i rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // 'phags pa'i bden pa rnams ni 'phags pa'i bden pa'i rang bzhin gyis stong // bsam gtan rnams ni

66b7('bum): snyoms par 'jug pa'i rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // rnam par thar pa rnams ni rnam par thar pa'i rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // mthar gyis gnas pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa rnams ni
66b8('bum): mthar gyis gnas pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa'i rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // rnam par thar pa'i sgo stong pa nyid dang / mtshan ma med pa dang / smon pa med pa ni rnam par
67a1('bum): thar pa'i sgo stong pa nyid dang / mtshan ma med pa dang / smon pa med pa'i rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // mngon par shes pa rnams ni mngon par shes
67a2('bum): pa'i rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // ting nge 'dzin rnams ni ting nge 'dzin gyi rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // gzungs kyi sgo rnams ni gzungs kyi sgo'i rang bzhin gyis sdong ngo // 
67a3('bum): bzhin gshegs pa'i stob sa ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs kyi rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // mi 'jigs pa rnams ni mi 'jigs pa rnams kyi rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // so
67a4('bum): so yang dag par rig pa rnams ni so so yang dag par rig pa'i rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // byams pa chen dpo ni byams pa chen po'i rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // snying
67a5('bum): rje chen po snying rje chen po'i rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa rnams ni sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa'i rang bzhin gyis stong ngo //

67a7('bum): phyir mi 'ong ba'i 'bras bu ni phyir mi 'ong ba'i 'bras bu'i rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // dgra bcom pa nyid ni dgra bcom pa nyid kyi rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // rang byang chub ni rang
67a8('bum): byang chub kyi rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // lam gyi rnam pa shes pa nyid ni lam gyi rnam pa shes pa nyid kyi rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // rnam pa thams cad mkhyen
67b1('bum): pa nyid ni rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // de nas tshe dang ldan pa sha ra dwa ti'i bus tshe dang ldan pa rab 'byor la 'di skad ces smras so//

67b4('bum): tshe dang ldan pa rab 'byor de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po yang 'di snyam du bdag gis bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon

112a1('bum): de skad ces bka' stsal pa dang / tshe dang ldan pa rab 'byor gyis/ bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das phyir mi ldog pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems

119a1('bum): mi khom pa brgyad po 'di dag gi nang du mi skye zhing / bud med du 'gyur ba yongasu mi 'dzin te/ rab 'byor rnam pa de dag dang / tshul de dag dang / mtshan ma de dag dang ldan pa'i/

128b1('bum): 'gyur ba lta ci smos te/ de ni gnas med do// mu stegs can dang kun tu rgyu ba gzhan dag la yid ches pas 'gro bar 'gyur ba la ci smos te/ de ni gnas med do// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'di ltar des ga
128b2('bum): yid ches pas 'gro ba'i chos gang yang yang dag par rje su mi mthong ste/ gzugs sam/ gzugs kyi de bzhin nyid yang dag par rjesu mi mthong ngo // tsher ba'am/ tshor ba'i de bzhin nyid yang dag

324a8('bum): cad mkhyen pa nyid du slob pa yin nam/ phyir mi 'ong ba'i 'bras bu 'dod chags dang bral bar bya ba'i phyir slob na/ rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du slob pa yin nam/ 
324b1('bum): phyir mi 'ang ba'i 'bras bu 'gag par bya ba'i phyir slob na/ rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du slob pa yin nam/ phyir mi 'ong ba'i 'bras bu mi skye bar bya b.ra'i phyir slob na rnam pa thams cad/ 
324b2('bum): mkhyen pa nyid du slob pa yin nas dgra bcom pa nyid zad par bya ba'i phyir slabo na rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du slob pa yin nam dgra bcom pa nyid
324b3('bum): 'dod chags dang bral bar bya ba'i phyir slob na rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du slob pa yin nas/ dgra bcom pa nyid 'gag par bya ba'i phyir slob na/ rnam
324b4('bum): pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du slob pa yin nam/ dgra pa bcom pa nyid mi skye bar ma smra bar bya ba'i phyir slob na/ rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du slob pa yin nam/ 
324b5('bum): rang byang chub zad par bya ba'i phyir slob na pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du slob pa yin nasarang byang chub 'dod chags dang bral bar bya ba'i phyir mngan/ 
324b6('bum): rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du slob pa yin nam/ rang byang chub 'gag par bya ba'i phyir sloban rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du slob pa yin nam
324b7('bum): rang byang chub mi skye bar bya ba'i phyir slob na rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du slob pa yin nam lam gyi rnam pa shes pa nyid zad par bya ba'i phyir slong na/ 
324b8('bum): rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du slob pa yin namalam gyi rnam pa shes pa nyid 'dod chags dang bral bar bya ba'i phyir slob na/ rnam pa
